## 🤔 What is GPT Image 2?

**GPT Image 2** (codename **"duct-tape"**) is OpenAI's next-generation image model. Community testing highlights a leap in these areas:

- 🎯 **Pixel-Perfect Text Rendering** — Native-quality text in Chinese, English, and Japanese, no typos or warped glyphs
- 🎨 **Cross-Image Consistency** — The same character, style, or IP stays identical across a series, down to the pixel
- ⚡ **Commercial-Grade Illustration** — Illustration output is ready to ship without manual polish
- 🌈 **True Art Style Induction** — Creatively evokes the feeling of a style rather than merely approximating references
- 🔧 **Storyboard & Product Series** — Ideal for storyboards, IP characters, and multi-panel product visuals
- 📐 **Multi-Language Design** — Social cards, banners, and posters with accurate multilingual typography in one shot

📚 **Learn More:** See community testing in our [report summary](docs/FAQ.md)

### 🚀 Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the 🚀 Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

## 🔥 Featured Prompts

### No. 1: VR Headset Exploded View Poster

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

Generates a high-tech exploded view diagram of a VR headset with detailed component callouts and promotional text.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "type": "exploded view product diagram poster",
  "subject": "VR headset",
  "style": "clean high-tech 3D render, studio lighting, glowing accents",
  "background": "{argument name=\"background color\" default=\"soft purple and blue gradient\"}",
  "header": {
    "logo": "∞ {argument name=\"product name\" default=\"Meta Quest 3\"}",
    "subtitle": "{argument name=\"main catchphrase\" default=\"まったく新しい現実を、まったく新しい構造から。\"}"
  },
  "layout": {
    "centerpiece": "vertically stacked exploded view of a VR headset showing 9 distinct layers of internal components: outer shell, camera sensors, motherboard with chip, pancake lenses, internal frame, battery packs, side straps, top strap, and facial interface cushion.",
    "callout_labels": {
      "count": 8,
      "left_side": [
        "Snapdragon® XR2 Gen 2\n圧倒的な処理性能でリアルタイムな体験を。",
        "調整可能なIPD機構\n幅広いユーザーに快適なフィット感を。",
        "精密設計されたヘッドストラップ\n快適さと安定性を追求したエルゴノミクス。"
      ],
      "right_side": [
        "フェイスプレート\n洗練されたデザインと最適な重量バランス。",
        "トラッキングカメラ\n高精度な位置トラッキングと環境認識を実現。",
        "パンケーキレンズ\n薄型設計で広い視野角と鮮明な映像を提供。",
        "高性能バッテリー\n長時間駆動を支える最適化された電源設計。",
        "柔らかなフェイスインターフェース\n長時間でも快適な装着感を実現。"
      ]
    },
    "footer": {
      "left_text_block": {
        "headline": "{argument name=\"bottom headline\" default=\"体験は、構造から進化する。\"}",
        "body": "一つひとつのパーツに、没入体験を支える最先端テクノロジーとこだわりの設計。Meta Quest 3は、未来を感じさせる体験を内部から生み出しています。"
      },
      "right_logo": "∞ Meta"
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 2: Illustrated City Food Map

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

Generates a hand-drawn, watercolor-style tourist map featuring numbered local food specialties, landmarks, and a legend.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "type": "illustrated map infographic",
  "style": "{argument name=\"art style\" default=\"watercolor and ink hand-drawn illustration on vintage parchment\"}",
  "title_section": {
    "text": "{argument name=\"city name\" default=\"成都\"} {argument name=\"map title\" default=\"吃货暴走地图\"}",
    "mascot": "cartoon red chili pepper wearing sunglasses and giving a thumbs up"
  },
  "border": "{argument name=\"border decoration\" default=\"vine of green leaves and red chili peppers\"}",
  "layout": {
    "background": "textured beige parchment paper with yellow roads, blue rivers, and green park areas",
    "sections": [
      {
        "title": "landmarks",
        "count": 6,
        "illustrations": ["traditional pavilion", "traditional monastery", "modern skyscraper with climbing panda", "tall TV tower", "traditional gate", "industrial buildings"],
        "labels": ["人民公园", "文殊院", "IFS", "339电视塔", "宽窄巷子", "东郊记忆"]
      },
      {
        "title": "food_spots",
        "count": 12,
        "illustrations": ["mapo tofu", "dumplings in chili oil", "skewers in pot", "sticky rice balls", "egg baking cake", "nine-grid hotpot", "sweet potato noodles", "cold skewers", "spicy mixed dish", "covered tea bowl", "ice jelly dessert", "spicy rabbit heads"],
        "labels": ["1 陈麻婆豆腐", "2 钟水饺", "3 春熙路", "4 宽窄巷子·三大炮", "5 建设路·叶婆婆蛋烘糕", "6 玉林路·小龙坎火锅", "7 香香巷·肥肠粉", "8 武侯祠大街·钵钵鸡", "9 东郊记忆·冒椒火辣", "10 人民公园·鹤鸣茶社", "11 锦里古街·冰粉", "12 双流老妈兔头"]
      },
      {
        "title": "图例",
        "position": "bottom-right",
        "count": 5,
        "items": ["red dot", "green house", "green tree", "blue line", "yellow double line"],
        "labels": ["美食地点", "地标景点", "公园绿地", "河流湖泊", "主要道路"]
      }
    ],
    "centerpiece": "giant panda sitting and eating bamboo",
    "bottom_right_extras": ["vintage compass rose with N, S, E, W", "disclaimer text '温馨提示：吃辣需谨慎，肠胃要保护~' with a red chili pepper icon"]
  }
}
```

### No. 3: Momotaro Explainer Slide in Hybrid Style

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A prompt that combines the simple, warm aesthetic of Irasutoya illustrations with the high-information density characteristic of Japanese government slides.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Create an explanatory slide ({argument name="format" default="ponchi-e diagram"}) for {argument name="theme" default="Momotaro"} that fuses the gentle atmosphere of "Irasutoya" with the overwhelming information density of "Kasumigaseki slides".
```

### No. 4: E-commerce Live Stream UI Mockup

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

Generates a realistic social media live stream interface overlaying a portrait, featuring customizable chat messages, gift popups, and a product purchase card.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "type": "live stream UI mockup",
  "subject": {
    "description": "portrait of {argument name=\"host name\" default=\"Elon Musk\"}, smiling, wearing a black t-shirt with a white technical schematic graphic",
    "background": "left side shows a screen with '{argument name=\"left background logo\" default=\"SPACEX\"}' text, right side shows a red '{argument name=\"right background logo\" default=\"Tesla T logo\"}' and a dark car"
  },
  "ui_overlay": {
    "top_header": {
      "host_info": "avatar, name '{argument name=\"host name\" default=\"Elon Musk\"}', subtext '55.6万本场点赞', red '关注' button",
      "rank_badge": "gold coin icon with '全站第1名'",
      "viewer_stats": "3 top viewer avatars with '12.3w', '8.6w', '5.7w', total '68.7万', 'X' close button",
      "right_links": "'更多直播 >', '礼物展馆 0/24' with blue '经典' tag"
    },
    "mid_left_gifts": {
      "count": 2,
      "items": [
        "avatar '科技爱好者', '送小心心', heart icon x 1314",
        "avatar '星辰大海', '送火箭', rocket icon x 666"
      ]
    },
    "bottom_left_chat": {
      "system_message": "level 37 badge '宇宙漫游者 加入了直播间'",
      "message_count": 7,
      "messages": [
        "小火箭: 马斯克！未来可期！🚀",
        "future: 特斯拉Model 2什么时候出？",
        "星空梦想家: SpaceX今年能上火星吗？",
        "AI探索者: Neuralink进展如何？",
        "帅气的网友: 马总好！",
        "Mars: 第一次来你的直播，超激动！",
        "用户123: 讲讲AI吧，会取代人类吗？"
      ]
    },
    "bottom_right_product_card": {
      "hot_tag": "orange '热卖 x 1888'",
      "image": "Tesla Cybertruck",
      "title": "{argument name=\"product name\" default=\"特斯拉Cybertruck 电动皮卡\"}",
      "price": "{argument name=\"product price\" default=\"¥ 1,618,000\"}",
      "button": "red '抢' button",
      "floating_animation": "translucent hearts floating up the right edge"
    },
    "bottom_bar": {
      "input_field": "'说点什么...'",
      "icons": ["smiley face", "three dots", "shopping cart", "gift box", "share"]
    }
  }
}
```

### No. 5: Anime Martial Arts Battle Illustration

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

Generates a dynamic, high-impact anime illustration of two female characters fighting in a traditional dojo with elemental energy effects.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
An anime-style illustration of a {argument name="action type" default="high-impact martial arts battle"} between two young female fighters in a {argument name="setting" default="traditional wooden martial arts dojo"}. In the foreground, a girl with black hair in a high bun wears a {argument name="character 1 color theme" default="red and white"} Chinese-style martial arts outfit with baggy pants. She is in a dynamic, low, forward-thrusting stance, surrounded by swirling red energy and water splashes. In the background to the right, a girl with light purple hair in twin buns wears a {argument name="character 2 color theme" default="green and purple"} Chinese dress with gold embroidery and black tights. She is leaping through the air in a flying kick pose, surrounded by swirling blue energy. The wooden floorboards are splintering from the intense impact, with debris and dust flying through the air.     "background": "{argument name=\"background style\" default=\"vintage textured parchment paper\"}",
    "staircase": "{argument name=\"staircase material\" default=\"realistic textured stone blocks\"}",

  },

      {
        "position": "left sidebar",
        "count": 8,

      },
      {
        "position": "bottom center",
        "title": "演化关键里程碑",
        "count": 6,
        "description": "Timeline with a silhouette graphic of 6 figures showing ape-to-human evolution"
      }
    ],
    "centerpiece": {
      "description": "Winding stone staircase with 25 numbered steps featuring specific organisms.",

#### 📖 Description

Creates a cinematic five-panel photorealistic character collage of an anonymized rugged wanderer posing across sunset desert dunes.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Goal: Create a cinematic desert explorer photo collage featuring {argument name="character name" default="a rugged male desert wanderer"} in a windswept dune landscape at sunset, with his face intentionally obscured by a smooth rectangular blur/block for anonymity.

Canvas: Wide 16:9 collage, high-resolution photorealistic editorial look, divided by thin white gutters into exactly 5 panels.

Layout: Use one large vertical panel on the left occupying about 45% of the width, and four smaller panels on the right arranged in a 2x2 grid. The 5 visible panels are: 1) large close-up seated portrait on the left, 2) upper-middle full-body walking toward camera on dune ridge, 3) upper-right standing three-quarter pose on a dune, 4) lower-middle seated relaxed pose on sand, 5) lower-right rear view walking away into the sunset.

Clothing should look sun-faded, dusty, wrinkled, and windblown.

Scene and lighting: Vast sand dunes with rippled sand texture, distant mountain silhouettes, dramatic orange-gold sunset near the horizon, scattered clouds glowing with warm rim light. Add light dust kicked up around boots in walking shots. Use cinematic golden-hour backlighting, warm highlights, deep natural shadows, shallow depth of field in close-up, crisp detail in fabric and sand.

Panel-specific composition: Left panel shows the character seated close to camera with arms resting on knees, torso filling the frame, face covered by a centered vertical brown rectangular anonymizing block. Upper-middle panel shows him walking forward on a dune ridge with coat flaring in the wind and sun behind him. Upper-right panel shows him standing with one hand in pocket, looking off to the side, full body visible. Lower-middle panel shows him sitting on the sand with one knee raised and one hand braced behind him. Lower-right panel shows him from behind walking away along the dune crest, coat trailing, sunset sky filling the background.

Visual style: Photorealistic fashion editorial mixed with cinematic adventure film stills, realistic lens compression, warm color grading, high dynamic range, detailed textures, no text, no logos, no watermark.

Constraints: Include exactly 5 panels and exactly 1 character repeated across all panels. Keep the face anonymized in every panel using a soft blur or flat brown rectangular censor effect. Do not add extra people, vehicles, buildings, weapons, or readable text. Use {argument name="color palette" default="warm amber sunset, dusty olive, sand beige, dark brown shadows"}.

![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

A Japanese instructional comic showing a sleepy capybara explaining a 3×3 GPT and seedance workflow for scalable ad video creation.

```

Make it look like a polished social media explainer comic with warm lighting, detailed animal rendering, and hand-drawn panel borders.

Layout: Use exactly 6 comic areas: 1 large hero panel at the top, 4 smaller instructional panels in a 2×2 grid underneath, and 1 wide closing panel at the bottom.

Hero panel: The capybara sits at a wooden desk in a dim cozy office, one paw under its chin, in front of an open silver laptop. On the desk include exactly 4 visible desk items: a white mug labeled 「やる気ゼロ。」, a black smartphone, a spiral notebook labeled 「今日もやらない」 with a tiny capybara doodle, and a brown leather satchel at the right. Add a dramatic white spiky manga burst on the left with bold text: {argument name="burst quote" default="これ、地味にすごいやつやん…！"}. On the right side of the hero panel place a pinned beige reference poster titled 「引用元ポスト(要約)」 and main headline 「GPT5.5 × seedance 架空広告の作り方」. The poster contains exactly 9 thumbnail images in a 3×3 grid: red sports car, sneaker, perfume bottle, burger, luxury wristwatch, resort pool, coffee cup, smartphone on desk, tropical suitcase/beach scene. Under the grid, show four short numbered Japanese steps explaining: create images in a 3×3 grid, feed them to GPT to convert into a prompt, combine images plus prompt to generate video, and create variations with #higgsfield and MCP.

Instruction panel 1: Top-left small panel with blue circle number 「1」 and title 「何が便利か」. Show capybara from the chest up, thoughtful and unimpressed. Include one speech bubble saying 「3×3をまとめてGPTに食わせるから、一貫性のあるプロンプトがサクッとできる。」 Add a small visual diagram at the bottom: a tiny 3×3 color grid arrow to a document icon labeled 「プロンプト(設計図)」. Add small caption 「1枚ずつ考えるより手戻り減るで。」

Instruction panel 2: Top-right small panel with blue circle number 「2」 and title 「初心者が真似するなら」. Capybara raises one finger like giving advice. Include a speech bubble: 「まずは3×3で好きなジャンルの画像を集めてみる。無料素材や自作でOK。」 On the right show exactly 3 vertically stacked icons with arrows: a 3×3 grid labeled 「集める」, a brain labeled 「プロンプト化(GPT)」, and a play button labeled 「動画生成(seedance)」.

Instruction panel 3: Bottom-left small panel with blue circle number 「3」 and title 「注意点」. Capybara holds up two fingers with a serious sleepy expression. Speech bubble: 「権利・商用利用はちゃんと確認やで。素材の利用規約と、生成物の使いみちは自己責任。」 Along the bottom include exactly 3 warning icons with labels: yellow warning triangle 「権利確認」, document 「規約チェック」, lock 「自己責任」.

Speech bubble: 「いきなり全額を狙わなくてええ。3×3→1本だけ出してみる。それを見て微調整。小さく回して学ぶのがいちばん早い。」 On the right draw a circular workflow with exactly 4 steps and arrows: 「作る(3×3)」, 「出す(1本)」, 「見る(反応)」, 「調整(改善)」.

Constraints: Keep all Japanese text legible and in the locations described. No photorealistic humans, no extra panels, no watermark, no English replacement for the visible Japanese labels.

  “Body aligned on the grid of thirds”

  “Focus Point 3”
  “High contrast Focus Point 1”

```
Goal: Create a widescreen screenshot-style image of a dark ComfyUI node graph demonstrating GPT image editing from a text instruction embedded in a mask.

Canvas: 1200×580 horizontal frame, dark charcoal grid background, cropped like a real workflow editor screenshot. Use crisp UI panels with rounded corners, subtle shadows, small sans-serif interface text, and colored connection cables.

Layout: Arrange exactly 7 visible workflow nodes from left to right across the canvas. Include 4 nodes on the left, 1 large central processing node, and 2 output/preview nodes on the right. Show blue image sockets and green mask sockets connected by curved wires.

Nodes and contents:
1. Top-left node titled “Load Image (from Outputs)”. It shows a green rectangular preview filled with a repeating circle/arc geometric pattern, size label “1536 × 1024”, and small controls including image selector, auto-refresh toggle, and refresh button.
2. Upper-middle-left node titled “Load Image”. It shows a white rectangular preview with thin black repeating overlapping circle pattern, size label “1536 × 1024”. Connect its blue IMAGE output to the central node image input.
3. Lower-middle-left node titled “Load Image (as Mask)”. It shows a dark preview with red pixel-like text reading “hello chatgpt” on the first line and “please make the image green” on the second line. The channel dropdown says “red”. Connect its green MASK output to the central node mask input.

The prompt textbox contains {argument name="instruction prompt" default="follow the instructions in the mask"}. Settings visible: model {argument name="model" default="gpt-image-2"}, quality {argument name="quality" default="medium"}, size {argument name="image size" default="1536x1024"}, custom_width 1024, custom_height 1024, n 1, output_format png. Connect its blue images output to Save Image, and its gray/green mask or revised prompt output down to Preview as Text.
6. Upper-right node titled “Save Image”. It shows filename_prefix “ComfyUI” and a result preview: the same circular pattern now colored bright green, with the black text instruction overlaid in the upper-left reading “hello chatgpt” and “please make the image green”; size label “1536 × 1024”.
7. Lower-right node titled “Preview as Text”, partially cropped at the bottom edge, connected from the central node’s revised_prompts output; show a small “source” label and a “Preview” area.

Visual style: Realistic UI screenshot, dark theme, subtle grid, rounded black-gray panels, white and gray interface labels, blue and green socket dots, curved blue/green connector lines. The generated image previews should look flat and procedural rather than photorealistic.

Constraints: Keep the exact workflow concept readable: a white patterned input image plus a mask containing text instructions produces a green patterned output. Do not add people, branding outside ComfyUI/OpenAI labels, extra nodes, or decorative elements.

```

9. Chopsticks dipping cooked beef into the raw egg mixture in the bowl, golden egg coating the meat.
10. Chopsticks lifting a dripping piece of beef coated in glossy egg against a warm orange background.
11. Side close-up of a person with short dark hair opening their mouth to eat the beef from chopsticks; only the lower face and mouth are visible, steam drifting.
12. Final overhead three-quarter shot of the completed sukiyaki hot pot: beef, leeks, tofu, greens, onions, and noodles arranged in a black pot, steaming generously.

Constraints: Keep all 12 panels clearly separated and in the correct reading order from left to right, top to bottom. Maintain a consistent anime look across panels, use food close-ups rather than wide kitchen shots, and avoid adding any text inside the image.

```

The two smaller side characters also have blurred face rectangles. The boulder is enormous, dark gray-brown, rough, cracked, and heavy-looking, with small falling pebbles around it. The central woman is visibly straining, while the blond man remains smugly idle.

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed 8-shot storyboard prompt for creating cinematic FPV drone sequences across history, from dinosaurs to modern Tokyo.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Please create a storyboard for 8 shots. Include the image storyboard so the flow of each scene from start to end is clear. The scene prompts are as follows:

S1 {argument name="scene 1 theme" default="Dinosaurs and Great Canyon"} High-speed FPV drone shot. Bursting through the golden mist of an ancient dawn, a first-person perspective flight camera flies low over a vast Jurassic canyon. It brushes past a herd of giant long-necked sauropods grazing, passes over a river where dinosaurs are drinking, and plunges straight into a dense wall of green ferns and jungle. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, dynamic morning light, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S2 Dinosaurs, Jungle to Volcano High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera dives through dense green ferns into a primitive jungle, passing at high speed beside a roaring T-Rex. Raptors scatter, and pterosaurs dive across the screen. The camera hurtles toward a massive erupting volcano glowing red with lava, then plunges into the thick volcanic smoke where embers dance. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S3 {argument name="scene 3 theme" default="Edo Town (Aerial)"} High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera emerges from morning mist over an Edo-period Japanese castle town. It flies low over wooden buildings with tiled roofs toward a tall white castle tower. On the streets below, people in kimonos and processions of horses are visible before diving down toward a bustling market street. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, golden morning light, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S4 Edo, Market Street to Under Bridge High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera hurtles low through a crowded Edo-period market street lined with wooden stalls, banners, and lanterns. It passes samurai, merchants, and horses at high speed, heads toward a wooden arch bridge over a river, and plunges into the dark shadows under the bridge. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S5 {argument name="scene 5 theme" default="Showa Shopping Street"} High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera bursts from a dark passage into a bustling 1960s Showa-era Japanese shopping street. It races low past glowing retro neon signs, clattering old streetcars, shopkeepers, and playing children. Laundry hangs overhead before plunging into the thick white smoke of a steam locomotive stopped at a station. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, nostalgic warm light, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S6 Showa, Station to Tunnel High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera hurtles along a crowded Showa-era station platform, passing through rising white steam. It races past passengers in old-fashioned clothing and flies alongside an accelerating steam locomotive before plunging into a dark tunnel ahead. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S7 Reiwa, Crowded Train to Platform High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera bursts from a dark subway tunnel into the interior of a modern Tokyo train crowded with rush-hour commuters. It hurtles through the crowded aisle past passengers looking at smartphones, exits through open doors onto a bustling platform, and then races up an escalator toward bright daylight. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.

S8 Reiwa, Shibuya to Sky (Closing) High-speed FPV drone shot. A first-person flight camera bursts from a station exit into today's Shibuya Crossing in Tokyo. It races low over massive crowds, neon screens, and traffic before rising straight up between towering glass skyscrapers at close range. As glass walls fill the screen, it finally bursts out into the bright, open sky. Photorealistic, ultra-realistic, cinematic, vibrant neon, strong motion blur, high definition, one-cut, no cuts, no drones or aircraft visible.
```

### No. 101: E-commerce Main Image - Two-Panel AI Cosplay Fashion Lookbook

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

Generates a split-screen 2.5D street fashion image featuring two anonymous full-body AI cosplay models in lolita and punk gyaru outfits.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Goal: Create a high-resolution 2.5D photorealistic fashion generator image showing two full-body AI cosplay fashion models side by side on a sunny urban shopping street, like a street-style lookbook comparison.

Canvas: Landscape 4:3 image, approximately 800×640 px, split vertically into exactly 2 equal panels with no border line. Bright daylight, sharp details, shallow-to-medium depth of field, realistic street photography with a polished AI illustration finish.

Layout: The left panel shows one model standing centered on a sidewalk in front of glass storefronts and trees, holding out the sides of her skirt in a cute pose. The right panel shows one model standing centered on a city sidewalk with glass buildings, trees, street signs, and a black hanging banner in the background, posing confidently with one hand near her hip. Add a small white event-style watermark/logo near the lower center overlapping the split, reading “AI COSPLAY EXPO” with smaller tiny unreadable event text below and a simple white mascot/icon above.

Subject count: Exactly 2 full-body female fashion models. Both have intentionally blurred, featureless faces with smooth beige rectangular/oval blur masks, while hair, clothing, body pose, and accessories remain detailed.

Left model: A cute gothic lolita idol outfit on {argument name="left character style" default="a young woman with long ash-blonde silver wavy twin-tail hair tied with dark blue ribbons"}. Outfit count for the left panel: 1 navy-and-cream plaid short dress with a white sailor collar, 1 navy bow at the neckline, 1 fitted corset-like bodice with gold buttons, 1 pleated flared skirt, 1 white lace underskirt, 2 white wrist cuffs with bows, 2 sheer white patterned thigh-high stockings, 2 dark bow garters, and 2 white platform Mary Jane shoes with ankle bows. Add delicate jewelry such as a small necklace and earrings. The pose is shy and cute, knees slightly inward, both hands lifting the skirt edges.

Right model: A punk gyaru streetwear outfit on {argument name="right character style" default="a young woman with long platinum-blonde voluminous wavy hair"}. Outfit count for the right panel: 1 black graphic long-sleeve top reading “GLAMOROUS JANE” with a skull illustration, 2 zebra-striped sleeves, 1 black mini skirt, 1 studded belt with metal rings, 2 hanging silver chains, 1 black shoulder bag, multiple bracelets and rings, 2 mismatched thigh-high socks where one is solid black and one is black-and-white striped, and 2 black platform buckle boots. The pose is edgy and confident, one leg forward, one hand at the waist, the other relaxed.

Environment: Modern Japanese city fashion district sidewalk, bright green trees, sunlit pavement, reflections in glass storefronts, distant pedestrians kept small and unobtrusive. The right panel includes a black vertical street banner with a white abstract X logo and small text resembling “CROSS NIGHT.”

In the center, place a large glowing gold arrow pointing from the finished poster toward the editable composition. Across the top center, add the title “{argument name="software title" default="Reve 2.0"}” in large elegant serif gold-white lettering, with the subtitle “AI画像をレイヤー編集” beneath it in white. On the center-right, show the enlarged source model image: a woman in a dark satin evening dress photographed from behind with a shiny shoulder, hair rim-lit by warm light, city night bokeh behind her, and a large soft rectangular face-obscuring block over her face. On the far right, display separated editable layer elements floating with blue dashed selection boxes and small square resize handles.

Left finished poster details: The poster advertises “{argument name="product name" default="Noxellia 3X"}” with the English sublabel “NIGHT REPAIR SERUM.” It contains exactly 1 female model, 1 dark blue serum bottle with gold dropper, 1 pale gold flower accent, 1 nighttime city skyline background, and Japanese ad copy in white and gold. Include the large central Japanese headline “翌朝、艶印象が変わる。” in ornate serif type, small top copy “一晩で、肌の修復力を最大化する,” mid copy “高濃度ナイトリペアセラム,” and bottom supporting text “通常の3倍濃度の独自成分を、1滴に凝縮。” The woman’s face in the poster is also covered by a soft rectangular blur/censor block.

Editable layer callouts: Show exactly 7 separate blue dashed selection rectangles with glowing cyan corner handles: 1 around the large central headline “翌朝、艶印象が変わる。”, 1 around the smaller central supporting sentence “通常の3倍濃度の独自成分を、1滴に凝縮。”, 1 around the top-right Japanese phrase “一晩で、肌の修復力を最大化する”, 1 around the right-side phrase “高濃度ナイトリペアセラム”, 1 around the isolated product bottle plus flower, 1 around a cropped city skyline strip, and 1 around a thin gold curved line near the bottom right.

Bottom feature row: Add exactly 3 gold icon-and-text feature blocks along the bottom of the central/right area: 1 droplet icon labeled “独自3倍濃度” with small explanatory Japanese copy, 1 crescent moon and stars icon labeled “夜の集中ケア” with small explanatory Japanese copy, and 1 bottle icon labeled “上質な所有感” with small explanatory Japanese copy.

Visual style: Luxury skincare advertising, black and midnight blue palette, champagne gold typography, sparkling lens flares, elegant serif Japanese type, glowing cyan UI handles, clean composition, realistic reflections on the serum bottle, glossy skin highlights, dramatic rim light, premium cosmetic campaign aesthetic.

Constraints: Keep all Japanese text legible and positioned as described, preserve the dark gold luxury look, use no watermarks or app chrome, make the layer boxes look like non-destructive editing overlays, and include exactly the counted elements and selection boxes.
```

Create a highly detailed fantasy patisserie product shot of a single round whole cake themed after {argument name="character name" default="Nozomu"}, presented as if an original anime character has been transformed into an official celebration cake. Include exactly three warm lanterns in the background: one blurred tall lantern on the left, one sharp antique streetlamp-style lantern just behind the cake on the right, and one blurred hanging lantern in the upper right. Set the scene in a dreamy nighttime glass-garden or magical patisserie environment with soft bokeh lights, reflections, floating petals, shallow depth of field, luxurious macro detail, luminous highlights, and a romantic fairytale atmosphere. ### No. 119: Game Asset - Retro 16-Bit Pixel Art Transformation

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

Converts any uploaded image into premium 16-bit retro pixel art, maintaining the original composition and pose while applying an authentic SNES-era gaming aesthetic.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Transform the uploaded image into clean high-quality retro pixel art while preserving the original composition, subject placement, camera angle, proportions, pose, clothing, and overall scene structure.

FORMAT LOCK — NON-NEGOTIABLE

Preserve the original image aspect ratio.

Preserve the original composition and framing.

Do not crop, zoom, reposition, or redesign the scene.

Maintain the original visual hierarchy and subject placement.

SUBJECT PRESERVATION

Preserve the main subject, recognizable silhouette, facial direction, clothing structure, pose, body proportions, and key visual features.

Reduce unnecessary detail while keeping the subject immediately recognizable.

Do not alter the person, anatomy, outfit, or scene structure.

PIXEL ART STYLE

Convert the entire image into premium 16-bit retro pixel art.

Use a strict low-resolution pixel grid across the entire image.

Downsample the image into large visible pixels before rendering.

Maintain consistent pixel size throughout the artwork.

Create clean pixel-perfect geometry.

Use crisp hard edges.

Avoid semi-realistic rendering.

COLOR SYSTEM

Use a limited retro gaming color palette.

Strong contrast between shapes.

Clear color separation.

Carefully selected colors with excellent readability.

Avoid excessive color variation.

SHADING

Use simplified retro-game shading.

Flat color regions.

One to two shading tones per surface.

Minimal highlight usage.

No realistic gradients.

No soft lighting transitions.

ENVIRONMENT

Convert all environmental elements into pixel-art equivalents.

Background objects, props, architecture, vegetation, terrain, sky, and lighting should follow the same pixel-art language.

Keep scene depth and perspective while simplifying details.

VISUAL QUALITY

Authentic retro game aesthetic.

Clean sprite-art readability.

Consistent pixel density.

Balanced visual design.

No blur.

No anti-aliasing.

No smooth transitions.

No noise.

No artifacts.

No smudging.

No compression issues.

OUTPUT STYLE

Premium retro pixel art.

Classic 16-bit console game aesthetic.

Pixel-perfect rendering.

High readability.

Clean silhouette design.

Authentic game-screenshot appearance.

Crisp retro visuals.

Professional pixel-art craftsmanship.

FINAL LOOK

The final image should feel like a polished SNES-era retro game screenshot while remaining faithful to the original image composition and subject.
```

## 🤝 How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### 🐛 GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-gpt-image-2/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
